***фраер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фра́ер</a> (14081)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>There are a number of theories about the origin of this term:
</p>
<ul><li>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Freier</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">suitor, bachelor; customer of prostitutes</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">frei</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">free</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First used by prostitutes in Odessa's criminal world to refer to their clients.</li>
<li>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Freiherr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">baron</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">frei</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Herr</i>.</li>
<li>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">פֿרײַער</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">frayer</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">free person</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">פֿרײַ</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fray</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">free</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Referring to someone who has not served time in prison.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фра́ер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">frájer</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фра́ера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фраера́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фра́еры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фраеро́в</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фра́еров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> not a criminal person, a potential victim of a crime, any person (male); a person criminals may consider as deserving of respect, even if he doesn't belong to their group.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фра́ер</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:устремляться.html>устремля́лся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сто́рону</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:беда.html>беды́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свое́й</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">I <b>frájer</b> ustremljálsja v stóronu bedý svojéj.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">And the guy just went towards his trouble</span></dd></dl></div> ("<i><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:солнечный.html>со́лнечной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>стороне́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лицы</a></i>", <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дина.html>Ди́на</a> Рубина</b>)</dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вор.html>вор</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:честный.html>че́стный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фра́ер</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja ne vor, ja čéstnyj <b>frájer</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I'm not a thief, I'm an honest bloke</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> an unpleasant person, e.g. someone who behaves arrogantly, spoils a party, etc.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жадность.html>жа́дность</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фра́ера</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:погубить.html>погу́бит</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Žádnostʹ <b>frájera</b> pogúbit.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Greed will kill the bad guy.</span></dd></dl></div> (<i>saying</i>)</dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́тот</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фра́ер</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:соизволить.html>соизво́лил</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:позвонить.html>позвони́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хотя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:названивать.html>назва́нивал</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:течение.html>тече́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несколько.html>не́скольких</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дней</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Étot <b>frájer</b> dáže ne soizvólil mne pozvonítʹ, xotjá ja jemú nazvánival v tečénije néskolʹkix dnej.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">And this jerk didn't even condescend to call me, although I kept calling him for a few days.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A naive or inexperienced person, a sucker, mug, patsy or sap; one who accedes to all requests, and is easily taken advantage of.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>Бог</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:фраер.html>фра́ер</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́дит</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Box ne <b>frájer</b>, on vsjó vídit.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">God is not a sucker, he sees everything.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

Зализняка).

***франт.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:франт.html>франт</a> (22735)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">frant</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rogue, clown, comedian</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from a diminutive of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">František</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">given name</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***фронт.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фронт.html>фронт</a> (923)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Front</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фронт.html>фронт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">front</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фронт.html>фро́нта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фронт.html>фронты́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фронт.html>фронто́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> front <i>(large operational military command that controls several armies; equivalent to U.S. army group)</i></li>
<li>battle front, front line</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фронтон.html>фронто́н</a> (28475)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">fronton</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">frontone</i>.

***фу.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фу.html>фу</a> (6992)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фу.html>фу</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fu</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>pew!, ew!, yuck! (it stinks!)</li>
<li>aw! (mild disappointment)</li>
<li><i>(a command for a dog)</i> stop that!, don't do that!</li></ol>

***фужер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фужер.html>фуже́р</a> (12763)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Late 19th century after <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">verre de fougère</i>, a <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.lareveillee.org/wp-content/uploads/2010/02/Le-verre-de-foug%C3%A8re-dans-Circulaire-n%C2%B0116-de-d%C3%A9cembre-20151.pdf">certain quality grade</a> of wine glasses, made from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">fougère</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fern</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> ash, manufactered particularly in the town <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">Fougères</i> having its name from abundance in fern and later a glassware industry by reason of this fern presence.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фужер.html>фуже́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fužér</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фужер.html>фуже́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фужер.html>фуже́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фужер.html>фуже́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tall wine glass</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:фу.html>фу</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>же́р</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-фужер-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фундамент.html>фунда́мент</a> (6988)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">fundamentum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">foundation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***фуражка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фуражка.html>фура́жка</a> (3392)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">forage cap</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Kozma_Kryuchkov.jpeg/220px-Kozma_Kryuchkov.jpeg" decoding="async" width="220" height="291" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Kozma_Kryuchkov.jpeg/330px-Kozma_Kryuchkov.jpeg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/77/Kozma_Kryuchkov.jpeg/440px-Kozma_Kryuchkov.jpeg 2x" data-file-width="781" data-file-height="1033" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:фуражка.html>фура́жка</a></div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фуражка.html>фура́жка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">furážka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фуражка.html>фура́жки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фуражка.html>фура́жки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фуражка.html>фура́жек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">British</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> peaked cap, combination cap, forage cap</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> service cap, wheel cap, combination cover</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фургон.html>фурго́н</a> (5106)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">fourgon</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фургон.html>фурго́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">furgón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фургон.html>фурго́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фургон.html>фурго́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фургон.html>фурго́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>portable loading room, van, caravan, wagon, waggon, camion <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a covered vehicle used for carrying goods</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2018</b> December 29,  “<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:корова.html>коро́ва</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбежать.html>сбежа́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> скотобо́йни <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:попасть.html>попа́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:вегетарианский.html>вегетариа́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рай.html>рай</a>»</span>”, in  <cite>Lenta.ru</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://lenta.ru/news/2018/12/29/cow/">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сша.html>Сша</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:корова.html>коро́ва</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самостоятельный.html>самостоя́тельно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выбраться.html>вы́бралась</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:фургон.html>фурго́на</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грузовик.html>грузовика́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:вёзший.html>вёзшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:животный.html>живо́тных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> скотобо́йню, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбежать.html>сбежа́ла</a>.</span></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">V SŠA koróva samostojátelʹno výbralasʹ iz <b>furgóna</b> gruzoviká, vezševo živótnyx na skotobójnju, i sbežála.</span></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">In the USA a cow got out of the <b>waggon</b> of a lorry that delivered animals to slaughter, and fled.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
